 bhartiya vetalifting sangh doping ke kilaaf lagaataar sakhti kaa rukh dikhaa rahi he
 It has also decided to impose a 2-year ban on 8 coaches whose players have been found guilty of doping
 yahi nahin is khel sangh ne dilli, punjab, haryana or manipur jaise rajyon par bhi ek saal kaa pratibandh lagane kaa faisalaa kiya he
 Because, players from these states have been found guilty of the highest number of doping
 lekin wo ye bhi kehete hai ki chaahe sabhi rajyon par pratibandh lagaana pade, wo doping ke kilaaf lagaataar sakht faisale lete rahenge
 This year, 26 weightlifter have been found guilty of doping
 bhartiya vetalifting sangh ke upaadhyaksh sahadev yadav maanate hai ki ye sankhya badi he
 But he also clarifies about the punishment that Nada (national Anti Doping Agency) will decide the period of punishment
 sahadev yadav ne itnaa zarur bataaya ki jin rajyon ko suspend kiya gaya he unhen dedh lakh rupee kaa jurmaana dena padegaa
 Apart from this, if the weightlifters are found guilty, the states will have to pay a fine of Rs 50,000 for the players
 unhone ye bhi saafe kiya kii coach kii sazaa ko lekar koi riyaayat nahin barti jaaegi
 The coach will not have to pay any amount as penalty
 dilli ke teen coach- virendra kumaar, ravi kumaar or esake bakshi ko do saal ke liye suspend kiya gaya he jabaki manipur ke 2 or madhya pradesh, punjab or odisha ke ek-ek coach ko bhi suspend kiya gaya he
 All these players have been found guilty of doping outside domestic competitions and competitions
 inhen neshnal youth games, junior championshipss, vishvavidhyalay, police games or railway kii pratiyogitaaon ke dauraan doping kaa doshi paaya gaya
 Sahadev Yadav, vice-president of the Indian Weightlifting Association, says that more and more weightlifters are being investigated these days, so many weightlifters are being caught
 wo kehete hai ki in dinon wo qareeb 500 sampling karavaate hai
 These investigations are being carried out from school games to national games and competitions
 wo ye bhi kehete hai ki kai coach khilaadiyon ko laalach dete hai taaki wo doping kar apana pradarshan behatar kar medal jeet saken
 The comments unka kahana he ki medal kii jeet ke saath badi inami raqam kaa elaan bhi khilaadiyon kaa laalach badha detaa he
 For example, he says that if the players win a gold medal in the Commonwealth Games, they get around Rs 1 crore as a reward
 rio olympix kii taiyaariyon ko lekar sahadev yadav kehete hai ki taiyaari kii disha thik he
 If no player is injured then the team can bring good results
 khaaskar ravi (77 kilogram), satish kumaar (77 kilogram) or sanjeeta chanhu (48 kilogram) or mira bai (48 kilogram) or youth olympic games ke rajat padak vijeta regala venkat rahul (77 kilogram) jaise khilaadiyon se khaas ummid he
 Not only this, the sports association has also decided to impose a one-year ban on states like Delhi, Punjab, Haryana and Manipur
 kyonki, in rajyon ke khilaadi sabase zyaada sankhya main doping ke doshi paae gayi hai
 But they also say that even if all the states have to ban, they will continue to take strict decisions against doping
 is saal abtak 26 vetaliftor doping ke doshi paye gayi hai
 Sahdev Yadav, vice-president of the Indian Weightlifting Association, believes that these numbers are large
 lekin wo isaki sazaa ko lekar ye bhi saafe karte hai ki sazaa kii avadhi nadaa (neshnal anti doping agency) hi tay karegi
 Sahadev Yadav said so much that the states which have been suspended will have to pay a penalty of Rs 1
5 lakh
 iske alaava vetaliftron ke doshi paye jane par rajyon ko khilaadiyon ke liye 50,000 rupee kaa jurmaana bharna hoga
 He also clarified that no concession will be taken regarding the punishment of the coach
 coach ko jurmaane ke taur par zarur koi raqam adaa nahin kerani hogi
 Three coaches of Delhi - Virendra Kumar, Ravi Kumar and SK Bakshi have been suspended for two years while 2 coaches from Manipur and one each from Madhya Pradesh, Punjab and Odisha have also been suspended
 ye sabhi khilaadi gharelu pratiyogitaaon or pratiyogitaaon ke baahar doping ke doshi paae gayi hai
 They were found guilty of doping during national youth games, junior championships, varsity, police games and railway competitions
 bhartiya vetalifting sangh ke upaadhyaksh sahadev yadav bataate hai ki in dinon zyaada se zyaada vetaliftron kii jaanch karwaai ja rahi he, isliye kai vetaliftor pakade ja rahe hai
 They say that these days they conduct around 500 samples
 ye jaanch skool games se lekar neshnal games or pratiyogitaaon ke baahar bhi karwaai ja rahi he
 They also say that many coaches lure players so that they can improve their performance by doping and win medals
 tippaniyan He says that with the victory of the medal, the announcement of big prize money also increases the greed of the players
 udhaaharan ke taur par wo kehete hai ki agar khilaadi kaamanwealth khelon main swarna padak jitate hai to unhen qareeb 1karod rupee inaam ke taur par mil jate hai
 Regarding the preparations for the Rio Olympics, Sahadev Yadav says that the direction of preparation is right
 agar koi khilaadi ghayal nahin hua to team achche nattejey laa sakati he
 Players like Ravi (77 kg), Satish Kumar (77 kg) and Sanjita Chanhu (48 kg) and Meera Bai (48 kg) and Youth Olympic Games silver medalist Regala Venkat Rahul (77 kg) are expected to be special

 '' If Bharat Ratna Sachin Tendulkar and Lata Mangeshkar are part of a function in which the Chief Minister of another state is coming to attend, then the protocol of both the celebrities will be bigger than the Chief Minister
 agar yah program rajyapal or mukhyamantri ke sambandhit rajya main hi ho rahaa ho to is sthiti main hi sachin tendulkar or lata mangeshkar kaa protocol unase kam hoga
 In fact, not only Sachin or Lata Mangeshkar, all persons decorated with Bharat Ratna also get special protocol facilities
 rajyon se baahar ke kisi kaarykram main sambandhit rajyapal or mukhyamantri kaa protocol unase ek seedhi kam ho jaataa he, jabaki rajya main rahane par protocol ek seedhi upar rahata he
 Thus, the protocol of Sachin Tendulkar and Lata Mangeshkar is weakened as soon as the Governor and Chief Minister of Maharashtra leaves their state
 darasal, raashtrapati sachivalay kii ore se mananeeyon or anya sanvaidhanik padon par baithe ganmaanya vyaktiyon ke liye ek variyata kram nirdhaarit kiya gaya he
 Which is called the Table of President
 isamen kisi samaaroh ke liye padon kaa protocol tay kiya gaya he
 Celebrities who have received the Bharat Ratna, the country's highest honor, also have special protocol facilities
 aisi hastiyon ko protocol ke variyata kram kii 7-A shrenee main rakhaa gaya he
 While above them are President (1), Vice President (2), Prime Minister (3), Governor (4), Former President (5), Deputy Prime Minister (6), Chief Justice of Supreme Court and Speaker of Lok Sabha (6), The protocol of the Union Minister, Chief Minister (in his state), Deputy Chairman of NITI Aayog, former Prime Minister and Leader of Opposition in Lok Sabha and Rajya Sabha is above the Bharat Ratna at number seven
 inase upar hote hai bharat ratnarajyapal or mukhyamantri kaa protocol unke rajya main adhik majboot hota he, jabaki duusare rajya main jane par kamjor ho jaataa he
 Looking at the table shows that if the Chief Minister is in his state then his protocol is at number seven, while when he is out of the state, his protocol is at number eight
 isi tarah se agar rajyapal apane rajya ke kisi samaaroh main hai to unka protocol raashtrapati, uparashtrapati, pradhanmantri ke thik baad chauthe number par hota he, magar rajya se baahar hone par unka bhi protocol aathve number par pahunch jaataa he

 -rape ke kai mukademon main jaldi nyaay na milane se bhi halaat bigade hai?ham sarkari vakeelon kii merit ke hisaab se tainaati kar rahe hai
 They appoint them on the basis of points such as the preference of lawyers, the manner of lobbying in the cases, the style, the character
 sarkaar yah yojana bana rahi he ki in vakeelon ko sarkari maamalon kii pairvi ke liye alag se prashikshan diya jaae
 The government has also included the District Magistrate and District Judge in the selection of government lawyers
 yah teen vakeelon kaa panel banaakar shashan main bhejte hai jahaan se antim nirnay liya jaataa he

 sarkaar 218 nae fast trek court kholane ja rahi he
 Of these, 144 courts will hear cases of rape only from women
 abhi tak in court main mahilaon se jude anya maamle bhi aate the ab sirf rape ke hi maamle 144 court sunenge

 sarkaar ne tay kiya he ki rape ke maamle main turant chargeshit lage

 iske alaava sau nae pad atirikt satr nyaayadhish str ke bhi srujit kiye gaye hai
 110 family courts have also been opened to handle women's domestic affairs
 25 nae fast trek court essi-asti ke mukademon kii jald sunwaayee ke liye khole gaye hai

 saamanyatya kammertial mukademe civil nyaayalayon chalate the

 iesai kii madad se aatanki hamalon ko anjaam de rahaa he

 mumbai ke 26 / 11 hamale ke saboot die gaye, unka kya kiya bataaen

 jediu netaa kasee tyaagi ne palatwaar karte hue kaha ki aatankwaad ko pryojit karne vaale pakistan ke khilaaf hameshaa se saboot rahe hai

 imran khan ke bayaan se saaf he ki pakistan yuddh kii raah par chal rahaa he

 paak sainikon ke mansoobey bharat virdohi rahe hai, kashmir main aatankwaad failaane kaa kaam karte rahe hai

 aise main pakistan piem ke bayaan par hansi aa sakati he

 pakistan ke 65 or 71 main tukade tukade hue

 unhone kaha ki bharat duniya kii sabase badi takaton main se ek he
 This India is not the India of 62 this is the India of 2019

 ek to kootnithik tareeke se use alag-thalag karnaa hi sabase badi sajaa he

 pakistan kaa bayaan vahi ghisa pita he

 Karnataka Governor HR Bhardwaj on Friday appointed Congress Legislature Party leader Siddaramaiah as the Chief Minister of the state
 64 varshiya siddharmaiya somvaar ko pad evam gopneeyata kii shapath le sakate hai
 a release from the Raj Bhavan said, "the Governor is pleased to appoint Siddaramaiah as the Chief Minister of Karnataka
 " After meeting Bhardwaj, Siddaramaiah said that the Governor has invited him to take oath soon
 raaj bhawan ke baahar siddharmaiya ne samvaadadaataaon se kaha, "sambhavat: somvaar ko main mukhyamantri pad kii shapath luungaa
 " karnataka pradesh congress ke adhyaksh ji
 The appointment was made within three hours of meeting Siddaramaiah's voice after meeting the Governor of Parameshwara and informing him to invite the Congress Legislature Party leader to form the government
 saikadon samarthakon ke khushi manaane ke bich siddharmaiya ne kaha, "akele shapath lene ke baad main parameshwar ke saath nai dilli jaaunga or party adhyaksh sonia gandhi ke saath mil kar mantriparishad ke naam tay karuunga
 " isse pehle puure din raajnneetik ghatnakram chalaa
